# Text Elements
public class First {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        int x = 10, y = 20, z;
        z = x + y;
        String str = "Sum: ";
        System.out.print(str + z);
    }
} ^f91msbGi

--- ^zeXHHNlH

First.java

First.class ^8O7hntH8

Class Loading ^9bsuceuQ

new String("Sum:") ^pPrSF4Z6

Memory ^W2kzQEZR

- Class Loader will bring program from DISK to Main memory.
- Area where programs are kept, called as Method area.
- It is only keeping the methods. NO CLASSES.
- Interpreter/JIT compiler will interpret this code and get it executed.
- Normal variables, reference variable are kept inside stack.
- Literals are kept inside Method area or section inside Code section/ String POOL.
 ^zjKPzI1e

Interpreter/JIT ^kmVHyezI

Execution
ENGINE ^21QvXLY0

Native Method
Interface ^qdBKMi6h

Native Method
Libraries ^UxHOSEPT

Simplified version ^MGRwAcrK

Interpreter
JIT compiler
Garbage Collector ^FnEVxCea

Address of the program will be kept inside CPU
for execution. CPU will store the address of the next 
instruction to execute. Directly CPU is not executing.
JVM is involved. So JVM will take care of keeping the 
addresses of the next instructions to be executed and it
will pass it over to the CPU. So that's where PC registers
comes into play. More than 1 registers might be there depending 
on the  JVM ^xRRi1ipi

Class Loader Subsystem ^EePyq7OR
